###########################
# USA Events By herkles
###########################

add_namespace = ustates

country_event = { # Start up Event
	id = ustates.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.1 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.1.t
	desc = ustates.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_Continental_Map

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = ustates.1.a
		activate_mission = USA_help_economy_mission
	}
}

### Lead up to the Civil War ###
country_event = { # Black Monday hits America
	id = ustates.2
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.2 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.2.t
	desc = ustates.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_run_on_the_banks

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ustates.2.a
		add_stability = -0.1
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = USA_great_depression }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = USA_great_depression
				add_idea = USA_black_monday
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = USA_black_monday
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			HON = {
				country_event = {
					id = honduras.100
					days = 10
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # The Coalition Ticket?
	id = ustates.3
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.3 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.3.t
	desc = ustates.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Form the Coalition
		name = ustates.3.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = USA_civil_war
					option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_COMPROMISE_WITH_LONG_USA_VS_CSA
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -200
		hidden_effect = {
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = USA_conservative_democratic_power
				value = -1
			}
			set_country_flag = {
				flag = USA_coalition_strength
				value = 3
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_coalition_party
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				long_name = USA_coalition_long
				name = USA_coalition
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				long_name = USA_coalition_long
				name = USA_coalition
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				long_name = USA_coalition_long
				name = USA_coalition
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				long_name = USA_coalition_long
				name = USA_coalition
			}
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			country_event = { #Nominating Quentin Roosevelt
				id = ustates.8
				days = 85
			}
			country_event = { #Death of Big Bill Haywood
				id = ustates.20
				days = 110
			}
			country_event = { #Southern Democrats take umbrage
				id = ustates.4
				days = 125
			}
			country_event = { #Democrats v Republicans
				id = ustates.5
				days = 150
			}
			country_event = { #Coalition Rally
				id = ustates.6
				days = 175
			}
			country_event = { #Fighting between AFP and SPA politicians
				id = ustates.21
				days = 190
			}
			country_event = { #Huey Long Speaks
				id = ustates.19
				days = 200
			}
			country_event = { #Republicans v Olson's people
				id = ustates.7
				days = 215
			}
			country_event = { #Indian Citizenship Act
				id = ustates.9
				days = 235
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Don't form the coalition
		name = ustates.3.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = USA_civil_war
					option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_COMPROMISE_WITH_REED_USA_VS_TEX
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_no_coalition_party
			country_event = { #Increasing Radicalizing
				id = ustates.11
				days = 56
			}
			country_event = { #Olson's people flock to the SPA
				id = ustates.12
				days = 95
			}
			country_event = { #Death of Big Bill Haywood
				id = ustates.20
				days = 110
			}
			country_event = { #Democrat voters align with the AFP
				id = ustates.13
				days = 115
			}
			country_event = { #MacArthur speaks to Hoover
				id = ustates.14
				days = 153
			}
			country_event = { #The Battle of the Overpass
				id = ustates.15
				days = 185
			}
			country_event = { #Fighting between AFP and SPA politicians
				id = ustates.21
				days = 190
			}
			country_event = { #Huey Long Speaks
				id = ustates.19
				days = 200
			}
			country_event = { #Representatives Retiring
				id = ustates.16
				days = 215
			}
			country_event = { #Fighting between the SPA and AFP
				id = ustates.17
				days = 235
			}
		}
	}
}


### Coalition stuff
country_event = { # Southern Democrats take umbrage
	id = ustates.4
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.4 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.4.t
	desc = ustates.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = USA_coalition_party
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_election_1936_flag }
	}

	option = { # Let them Complain
		name = ustates.4.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = USA_civil_war
					option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_COMPROMISE_WITH_REED_USA_VS_TEX
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = USA_coalition_strength
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Force a compromise
		name = ustates.4.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 70
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.03
	}
}

country_event = { # Democrats v Republicans
	id = ustates.5
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.5 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.5.t
	desc = ustates.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_july4

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = USA_coalition_party
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_election_1936_flag }
	}

	option = { # side with the democrats
		name = ustates.5.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = USA_civil_war
					option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_COMPROMISE_WITH_REED_USA_VS_TEX
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = USA_coalition_strength
				value = -1
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.03
		}
	}
	option = { # Force a compromise
		name = ustates.5.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
		}
	}
	option = { # side with the republicans
		name = ustates.5.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = USA_civil_war
					option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_COMPROMISE_WITH_REED_USA_VS_TEX
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = USA_coalition_strength
				value = -1
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.1
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # The Coalition falls apart!
	id = ustates.10
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.10 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.10.t
	desc = ustates.10.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_Riots

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = USA_coalition_party
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = USA_coalition_strength
			value < 1
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_election_1936_flag }
	}

	option = {
		name = ustates.10.a
		add_stability = -0.15
		add_political_power = -100
		clr_country_flag = USA_coalition_party
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = -0.02
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat }
		remove_from_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
		remove_from_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
		remove_from_coalition = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				long_name = USA_social_democrat_party_long
				name = USA_social_democrat_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				long_name = USA_social_liberal_party_long
				name = USA_social_liberal_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				long_name = USA_market_liberal_party_long
				name = USA_market_liberal_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				long_name = USA_social_conservative_party_long
				name = USA_social_conservative_party
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_AFP_gains_strength
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SPA_gains_strength
		150 = {
			USA_increase_AFP_state_support = yes
		}
		371 = {

		}
		374 = {
			USA_increase_AFP_state_support = yes
		}
		375 = {

		}
		372 = {
			USA_increase_AFP_state_support = yes
		}
		370 = {
			USA_increase_AFP_state_support = yes
		}
		367 = {
			USA_increase_AFP_state_support = yes
		}
		364 = {
			USA_increase_AFP_state_support = yes
		}
		365 = {
			USA_increase_AFP_state_support = yes
		}
		366 = {
			USA_increase_AFP_state_support = yes
		}
		368 = {
			USA_increase_AFP_state_support = yes
		}
		363 = {
			USA_increase_AFP_state_support = yes
		}
		833 = {
			USA_increase_AFP_state_support = yes
		}
		395 = {
			USA_increase_SPA_state_support = yes
		}

### No Coalition Stuff
country_event = { # Increasing Radicalizing
	id = ustates.11
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.11 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.11.t
	desc = ustates.11.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_iww_demonstration

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = USA_no_coalition_party
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_election_1936_flag }
	}

	option = { # radicalization
		name = ustates.11.a
		add_stability = -0.15
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_AFP_gains_strength
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SPA_gains_strength
		368 = {
			USA_increase_AFP_state_support = yes
		}
		833 = {
			USA_increase_AFP_state_support = yes
		}
		359 = {
			USA_increase_SPA_state_support = yes
		}
		392 = {
			USA_increase_SPA_state_support = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { var = SPA_strength value = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { var = AFP_strength value = 1 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # The Battle of the Overpass
	id = ustates.15
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.15 FROM = [From.GetName]" }

	desc = ustates.15.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_workers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = USA_no_coalition_party
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_election_1936_flag }

country_event = { # The 1936 Election
	id = ustates.34
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.34 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.34.t

	desc = {
		text = ustates.34.d.coalition
		trigger = { has_country_flag = USA_coalition_party }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.34.d.default
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_coalition_party } }
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election }
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_election_1936_flag
			NIC = { country_event = { id = nic.40 days = 24 } }

			#next primaries
			country_event = { id = ustates.200 days = 1283 }
			country_event = { id = ustates.201 days = 1290 }
			country_event = { id = ustates.202 days = 1297 }
		}
	}

	option = { # Floyd Olson
		name = ustates.34.a
		trigger = { has_country_flag = USA_coalition_party }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = USA_civil_war
						option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_FOUR_SIDES
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = USA_civil_war
						option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_COMPROMISE_WITH_LONG_USA_VS_CSA
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		set_country_flag = USA_progressives_exist
		set_country_flag = USA_olson_was_president
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = {
				USA_Floyd_B_Olson_hog_sde
				USA_Cordell_Hull_for_mli
				USA_Jesse_Holman_Jones_eco_sde
				USA_Charles_Evans_Hughes_Sr_sec_sli
			}
			kill_ideology_leader = social_liberal
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Alf Landon"
				desc = "POLITICS_ALF_LANDON_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_USA_Alf_Landon_KR.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = social_liberal_subtype
				traits = {
					economic_reformer
				}
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
			last_election = "1936.11.8"
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.2
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_liberal }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			random_other_country = {
				news_event = { id = ustates.1001 days = 1 }
			}
			country_event = { id = ustates.36 days = 5 }
			country_event = { id = ustates.37 days = 5 }
			country_event = { id = ustates.39 days = 8 }
			country_event = { id = ustates.40 days = 54 }
			country_event = { id = ustates.64 days = 73 }
			LEC = {
				country_event = { id = lecyankded.3 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Jack Reed
		name = ustates.34.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = USA_civil_war
						option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_THREE_SIDES
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = USA_civil_war
						option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_KILL_LONG_USA_VS_CSA
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = USA_civil_war
						option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_KILL_REED_USA_VS_TEX
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = USA_civil_war
						option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_COMPROMISE_WITH_REED_USA_VS_TEX
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = USA_civil_war
						option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_COMPROMISE_WITH_LONG_USA_VS_CSA
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_coalition_party }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = SPA_strength
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		hidden_effect = {
			kill_ideology_leader = social_liberal
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Alf Landon"

				ideology = social_liberal_subtype
				traits = {
					economic_reformer
				}
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = syndicalist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
			last_election = "1936.11.8"
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_reed_was_president
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_all_ministers = yes

				USA_Jack_Reed_hog_syn
				USA_Eugene_Dennis_for_syn
				USA_Paul_Mattick_eco_syn
				USA_John_Abt_sec_syn
			}

country_event = { # Bounce event to determine success
	id = ustates.86
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.86 FROM = [From.GetName]" }

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #SUCCESS
		ai_chance = {
			base = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = USA_civil_war
					option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_THREE_SIDES
				}
			}
		}
		USA = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_assassinating_long }
				clr_country_flag = USA_assassinating_long
				set_country_flag = USA_assassinated_long
				set_country_flag = USA_can_purge_longists
				USA_disable_AFP_modifiers = yes
				news_event = ustates.87
				country_event = { id = ustates.89 days = 3 }
			}
			else = {
				clr_country_flag = USA_assassinating_reed
				set_country_flag = USA_assassinated_reed
				set_country_flag = USA_can_purge_syndicalists
				USA_disable_SPA_modifiers = yes
				news_event = ustates.88
				country_event = { id = ustates.90 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #FAILURE
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = USA_civil_war
						option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_KILL_LONG_USA_VS_CSA
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = USA_civil_war
						option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_KILL_REED_USA_VS_TEX
					}
				}
			}
		}
		USA = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_assassinating_long }
				clr_country_flag = USA_assassinating_long
				set_country_flag = USA_fails_to_kill_long_flag
				add_to_variable = { var = AFP_strength value = 2 }
				country_event = amcivwar.2
			}
			else = {
				clr_country_flag = USA_assassinating_reed
				set_country_flag = USA_fails_to_kill_reed_flag
				add_to_variable = { var = SPA_strength value = 2 }
				country_event = amcivwar.1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Victory for MacArthur
	id = ustates.116
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.116 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.116.t
	desc = ustates.116.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_usa_macarthur_speech

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # macarthur keeps power
		name = ustates.116.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				add = -20
				country_exists = PSA
				PSA = { NOT = { owns_state = 373 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -25
				country_exists = PSA
				PSA = { owns_state = 373 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = USA_post_civil_war_macarthur
					option = USA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_MACARTHUR_RESTORE_DEMOCRACY
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = macarthur_keeps_power_flag
		complete_national_focus = USA_american_caesar
		add_stability = -0.1
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.134
				days = 20
				random = 960
			}
			news_event = { id = worldnews.476 }
		}

	}
	option = { # MacArthur gives up power
		name = ustates.116.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				country_exists = PSA
				PSA = { NOT = { owns_state = 373 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 25
				country_exists = PSA
				PSA = { owns_state = 373 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = USA_post_civil_war_macarthur
					option = USA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_MACARTHUR_HOLD_ON
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		complete_national_focus = USA_democracy_triumphs
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = -0.15
		}
		country_event = { id = ustates.136 days = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			PSA = { country_event = { id = ustates.121 days = 10 random_days = 20 } }
			news_event = { id = worldnews.476 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # The great Migration
	id = ustates.134
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.134 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.134.t
	desc = ustates.134.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_Continental_Map

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = macarthur_keeps_power_flag
		OR = {
			country_exists = PSA
			country_exists = NEE
			CAN = {
				has_democratic_government = yes
				any_owned_state = {
					is_mainland_america = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = PSA }
			PSA = {
				save_event_target_as = migrate
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { country_exists = NEE }
			NEE = {
				save_event_target_as = migrate
			}
		}
		else = {
			CAN = {
				save_event_target_as = migrate
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # kill them
		name = ustates.134.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 70
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = USA_great_migration1
			days = 90
		}
		add_manpower = -5000
		add_war_support = 0.02
		add_stability = 0.02
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:migrate = {
				country_event = {
					id = ustates.135
					days = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Let them go
		name = ustates.134.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
		}
		add_war_support = -0.02
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = USA_great_migration2
			days = 50
		}
		add_manpower = -2500
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:migrate = {
				country_event = {
					id = ustates.135
					days = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Refugees from MacArthur(PSA)
	id = ustates.135
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.135 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.135.t

	desc = {
		text = ustates.135.d.let_go
		trigger = {
			USA = {
				has_idea = USA_great_migration1
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.135.d.army
		trigger = {
			USA = {
				has_idea = USA_great_migration2
			}
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_reconstruction

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Flavor
		name = ustates.135.a
		if = { # Big Mac let them go
			limit = {
				USA = {
					has_idea = USA_great_migration1
				}

country_event = { # Floyd Olson Passes Away
	id = ustates.185
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.185 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.185.t

	desc = {
		text = ustates.185.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Floyd Olson"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.185.d.senator
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Floyd Olson"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_floyd_olson

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ustates.185.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Floyd Olson"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -15
		kill_country_leader = yes
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_liberal
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Quentin Roosevelt"
			desc = "POLITICS_QUENTIN_ROOSEVELT_DESC"
			picture = "Portrait_USA_Quentin_Roosevelt.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = social_liberal_subtype
			traits = {
				appeaser
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Henry Wallace"
				desc = "POLITICS_HENRY_WALLLACE_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_USA_Henry_Wallace.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = social_democrat_subtype
				traits = {
					tenacious_negotiator
				}
			}
		}
		add_ideas = USA_Quentin_Roosevelt_hog_sli
	}
	option = {
		name = ustates.185.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Floyd Olson"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -5
		hidden_effect = {
			kill_ideology_leader = social_democrat
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Henry Wallace"
				desc = "POLITICS_HENRY_WALLLACE_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_USA_Henry_Wallace.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = social_democrat_subtype
				traits = {
					tenacious_negotiator
				}
			}
		}
	}
}


### 1940 Elections and Primaries ###
country_event = { # 1940 Progressive Primary
	id = ustates.200
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.200 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.200.t
	desc = ustates.200.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_progressives_exist
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Henry Wallace
		name = ustates.200.a
		set_country_flag = USA_1940_progressive_primary_wallace
	}
}

country_event = { # 1940 Republican Primary
	id = ustates.201
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.201 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.201.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	desc = {
		text = ustates.201.d.landon
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = { name = "Alf Landon" }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.201.d.not_elected
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Alf Landon" } }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # nominate Quentin Roosevelt
		name = ustates.201.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = { name = "Alf Landon" }
				PSA = { has_country_flag = PSA_restored_roosevelt }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1940_republican_primary_roosevelt
	}
	option = { # re-nominate Alf Landon
		name = ustates.201.b
	}
	option = { # Douglas Macarthur
		name = ustates.201.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = Douglas_MacArthur_dead
				has_country_leader = { name = "Alf Landon" }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1940_republican_primary_macarthur
	}
}

country_event = { # 1940 Democrat Primary
	id = ustates.202
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.202 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.202.t
	desc = { # Democratic Party has the Presidency
		text = ustates.202.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = { name = "John Nance Garner" }
		}
	}
	desc = { # Democratic Party does not have the Presidency
		text = ustates.202.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "John Nance Garner" } }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Wendell Willkie (liberal)
		name = ustates.202.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = { name = "John Nance Garner" }
				PSA = { has_country_flag = PSA_restored_willkie }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_willkie
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = USA_conservative_democratic_power
			value = -1
		}
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = USA_liberal_democratic_power
			value = 1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.170 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = { # John Nance Garner
		name = ustates.202.b
	}
	option = { # Harry F. Byrd
		name = ustates.202.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "John Nance Garner" } }
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_byrd
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = USA_conservative_democratic_power
			value = 1
		}
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = USA_liberal_democratic_power
			value = -1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.169 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1940 Election
	id = ustates.203
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.203 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.203.t
	desc = ustates.203.d.civil_war_happened
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			create_country_leader = { # Henry Wallace
				name = "Henry Wallace"
				desc = "POLITICS_HENRY_WALLLACE_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_USA_Henry_Wallace.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = social_democrat_subtype
				traits = {
					tenacious_negotiator
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_republican_primary_roosevelt }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Quentin Roosevelt"
					desc = "POLITICS_QUENTIN_ROOSEVELT_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Quentin_Roosevelt.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					traits = {
						appeaser
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_republican_primary_macarthur }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Douglas MacArthur"
					desc = "POLITICS_DOUGLAS_MACARTHUR_CIVILIAN_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Douglas_MacArthur_civilian.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					traits = {
						war_industrialist
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_willkie }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Wendell Willkie"
					desc = "POLITICS_WENDELL_WILLKIE_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Wendell_Willkie_KR.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = market_liberal_subtype
					traits = {
						appeaser
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_byrd }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Harry F. Byrd"
					desc = "POLITICS_HARRY_BYRD_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Harry_F_Byrd.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_conservative_subtype
					traits = {
						backroom_backstabber
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Republican
		name = ustates.203.a
		set_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		set_country_flag = USA_1940_election_republican
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_liberal
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Quentin Roosevelt
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_republican_primary_roosevelt }
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_Quentin_Roosevelt_hog_sli
					USA_John_Bassett_Moore_for_sli
					USA_Charles_Edison_eco_sli
					USA_Charles_Douglas_Jackson_sec_sli
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ustates.175
					days = 60
					random = 15840
				}
			}
			else_if = { # Douglas MacArthur
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_republican_primary_macarthur }
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_Douglas_MacArthur_hog_sli
					USA_John_Bassett_Moore_for_sli
					USA_Charles_Edison_eco_sli
					USA_Charles_Douglas_Jackson_sec_sli
				}
			}
			else = { # Alf Landon
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_Alf_Landon_hog_sli
					USA_John_Bassett_Moore_for_sli
					USA_Charles_Edison_eco_sli
					USA_Charles_Douglas_Jackson_sec_sli
				}
			}

			# next primaries
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.204
				days = 1283
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.205
				days = 1290
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.206
				days = 1297
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Democrat
		name = ustates.203.b
		set_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		set_country_flag = USA_1940_election_democrat
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_willkie }
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = market_liberal
				election_frequency = 48
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				popularity = 0.20
			}
			else = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_conservative
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
				set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
				add_to_coalition = yes
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_conservative
					popularity = 0.20
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Wendell Willkie
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_willkie }
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_Wendell_Willkie_hog_mli
					USA_Cordell_Hull_for_mli
					USA_Daniel_Calhoun_Roper_eco_mli
					USA_Alben_W_Barkley_sec_mli
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ustates.176
					days = 60
					random = 15840
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ustates.177
					days = 60
					random = 15840
				}
			}
			else_if = { # Harry F. Byrd
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_byrd }
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_Harry_F_Byrd_hog_sco
					USA_Cordell_Hull_for_mli
					USA_William_Daniel_Leahy_eco_sco
					USA_Martin_Dies_Jr_sec_sco
				}
			}
			else = { # John Nance Garner
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_John_Nance_Garner_hog_sco
					USA_Cordell_Hull_for_mli

					days = 60

				days = 1283

				days = 1290
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.206
				days = 1297
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Progressive
		name = ustates.203.c

		}

		set_country_flag = USA_1940_election_progressive

			has_government = social_democrat
		}
	}
	desc = { # Progressive Party does not have the Presidency
		text = ustates.204.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = social_democrat }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_progressives_exist
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Henry Wallace
		name = ustates.204.a
		set_country_flag = USA_1944_progressive_primary_wallace

	option = { # Philip La Follette
		name = ustates.204.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = social_democrat }

	}

	trigger = {
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # nominate Thomas Dewey
		name = ustates.205.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = social_liberal }
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1944_republican_primary_dewey
	}
	option = { # nominate Quentin Roosevelt
		name = ustates.205.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = social_liberal }
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1944_republican_primary_roosevelt
	}
	option = { # Re-nominate the President
		name = ustates.205.b
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_liberal
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1944_republican_primary_president
	}
}

country_event = { # 1944 Democrat Primary
	id = ustates.206
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.206 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.206.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	desc = { # Democratic Party has the Presidency
		text = ustates.206.d.president
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = social_conservative
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # Democratic Party does not have the Presidency
		text = ustates.206.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_conservative
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Richard Russell Jr.
		name = ustates.206.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_conservative
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_russell
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = USA_conservative_democratic_power
			value = 1
		}
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = USA_liberal_democratic_power
			value = -1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.169 days = 3 }
		}
	}
	option = { # Alben W. Barkley
		name = ustates.206.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_conservative
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_barkley
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = USA_conservative_democratic_power
			value = -1
		}
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = USA_liberal_democratic_power
			value = 1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.170 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = { # James E. Murray
		name = ustates.206.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_conservative
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_murray
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = USA_conservative_democratic_power
			value = -1
		}
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = USA_liberal_democratic_power
			value = 1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.170 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = { # re-nominate the President
		name = ustates.206.e
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = social_conservative
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_president
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Wendell Willkie"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = USA_conservative_democratic_power
				value = -1
			}
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = USA_liberal_democratic_power
				value = 1
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ustates.170 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = USA_conservative_democratic_power
				value = 1
			}
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = USA_liberal_democratic_power
				value = -1
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ustates.169 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1944 Election
	id = ustates.207
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.207 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.207.t
	desc = ustates.207.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_progressive_primary_follette }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Philip La Follette"
					desc = "POLITICS_PHILIP_LA_FOLLETTE_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Philip_La_Follette.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_democrat_subtype
					traits = {
						reluctant_interventionist
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_progressive_primary_follette }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Henry Wallace"
					desc = "POLITICS_HENRY_WALLLACE_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Henry_Wallace.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_democrat_subtype
					traits = {
						great_survivor
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_republican_primary_dewey }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Thomas Dewey"
					desc = "POLITICS_THOMAS_DEWEY_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Thomas_Dewey_KR.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					traits = {
						great_survivor
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = USA_1944_republican_primary_dewey
						has_country_flag = USA_1944_republican_primary_president
					}
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Quentin Roosevelt"
					desc = "POLITICS_QUENTIN_ROOSEVELT_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Quentin_Roosevelt.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					traits = {
						appeaser
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_murray }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "James E. Murray"
					desc = "POLITICS_JAMES_MURRAY_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_James_Murray.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = market_liberal_subtype
					traits = {
						tenacious_negotiator
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_barkley }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Alben W. Barkley"
					desc = "POLITICS_ALBEN_BARKLEY_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Alben_Barkley.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = market_liberal_subtype
					traits = {
						silent_workhorse
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_murray
						has_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_barkley
						has_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_president
					}
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Richard Russell Jr."
					desc = "POLITICS_RICHARD_RUSSELL_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Richard_Russell_Jr.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_conservative_subtype
					traits = {
						nationalist_symbol
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Progressive
		name = ustates.207.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_progressives_exist
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election
		set_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Philip La Follette
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_progressive_primary_follette }
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_Philip_La_Follette_hog_sde
					USA_Adolf_Augustus_Berle_Jr_for_sde
					USA_Hjalmar_Petersen_eco_sde
					USA_Konrad_Knute_Solberg_sec_sde
				}
			}
			if = { # Henry Wallace
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_progressive_primary_follette }
				}
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_Henry_Wallace_hog_sde
					USA_Hugh_Simons_Gibson_for_sde
					USA_Hjalmar_Petersen_eco_sde
					USA_Elmer_Austin_Benson_sec_sde
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ustates.179
					days = 60
					random = 15840
				}
			}

			# next primaries
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.209
				days = 1283
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.210
				days = 1290
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.211
				days = 1297
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.212
				days = 1304
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Republican
		name = ustates.207.b
		set_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election
		set_country_flag = USA_1944_election_republican
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_liberal
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Thomas Dewey
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_republican_primary_dewey }
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_Thomas_Dewey_hog_sli
					USA_John_Bassett_Moore_for_sli
					USA_Charles_Edison_eco_sli
					USA_Charles_Douglas_Jackson_sec_sli
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ustates.184
					days = 60
					random = 15840
				}
			}
			if = { # Quentin Roosevelt
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = USA_1944_republican_primary_dewey
						has_country_flag = USA_1944_republican_primary_president
					}
				}
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_Quentin_Roosevelt_hog_sli
					USA_John_Bassett_Moore_for_sli
					USA_Charles_Edison_eco_sli
					USA_Charles_Douglas_Jackson_sec_sli
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ustates.175
					days = 60
					random = 15840
				}
			}

			# next primaries
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.209
				days = 1283
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.210
				days = 1290
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.211
				days = 1297
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.212
				days = 1304
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Democrat
		name = ustates.207.c
		set_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election
		set_country_flag = USA_1944_election_democrat
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_russell }
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = social_conservative
				election_frequency = 48
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				popularity = 0.20
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_murray
					has_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_barkley
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = market_liberal
				election_frequency = 48
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				popularity = 0.20
			}
		}
		else = {
			increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_20 = yes
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # James E. Murray
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_murray }
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_James_E_Murray_hog_mli
					USA_Henry_Morgenthau_Jr_for_mli
					USA_Daniel_Calhoun_Roper_eco_mli
					USA_Alben_W_Barkley_sec_mli
				}
			}
			if = { # Alben W. Barkley
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_barkley }
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_Alben_W_Barkley_hog_mli
					USA_Henry_Morgenthau_Jr_for_mli
					USA_Daniel_Calhoun_Roper_eco_mli
					USA_Robert_Ferdinand_Wagner_I_sec_mli
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ustates.182
					days = 60
					random = 15840
				}
			}
			if = { # Richard Russell Jr.
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_murray
						has_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_barkley
						has_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_president
					}
				}
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_Richard_Russell_Jr_hog_sco
					USA_James_Watson_Gerard_Jr_for_sco
					USA_Dean_Gooderham_Acheson_for_sco
					USA_Martin_Dies_Jr_sec_sco
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ustates.183
					days = 60
					random = 15840
				}
			}

			# next primaries
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.209
				days = 1283
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.210
				days = 1290
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.211
				days = 1297
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.212
				days = 1304
			}
		}
	}

### 1948 Elections and Primaries ###
country_event = { # 1948 Progressive Party
	id = ustates.209
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.209 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.209.t
	desc = { # Progressive Party won the presidency just last time
		text = ustates.209.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_progressive }
		}
	}
	desc = { # Progressive Party won also in 1940
		text = ustates.209.d.president_steps_down
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive
			has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_progressive
		}
	}
	desc = { # Progressive Party does not have the Presidency
		text = ustates.209.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = social_democrat }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_progressives_exist
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1948_election }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Philip La Follette
		name = ustates.209.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_government = social_democrat }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive }
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_progressive
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1948_progressive_primary_folette
	}
	option = { # Glen H. Taylor
		name = ustates.209.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_government = social_democrat }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive }
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_progressive
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1948_progressive_primary_taylor
	}
	option = { # Keep the Presidency
		name = ustates.209.c
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_progressive }
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1948_progressive_primary_president
	}
}

	id = ustates.210
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.210 FROM = [From.GetName]" }

	desc = { # Republican Party won the presidency just last time
		text = ustates.210.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_liberal
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_republican }
		}
	}
	desc = { # Republican Party won also in 1940
		text = ustates.210.d.president_steps_down
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_liberal
			has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_republican
		}
	}
	desc = { # Republican Party does not have the Presidency
		text = ustates.210.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = social_liberal }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1948_election }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Thomas Dewey
		name = ustates.210.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_government = social_liberal }
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_republican
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1948_republican_primary_dewey
	}
	option = {
		name = ustates.210.f
		trigger = {
			country_exists = PSA
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_government = social_liberal }
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_republican
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1948_republican_primary_rooseveltII
	}
	option = { # Earl Warren
		name = ustates.210.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { country_exists = PSA }
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_government = social_liberal }
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_republican
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1948_republican_primary_warren
	}
	option = { # Charles L. McNary
		name = ustates.210.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = PSA
				PSA = { has_country_flag = PSA_restored_mcnary }
			}
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_government = social_liberal }
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_republican
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1948_republican_primary_mcnary
	}
	option = { # President is re-elected
		name = ustates.210.e
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_liberal
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_republican }
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1948_republican_primary_president
	}
}

country_event = { # 1948 Liberal Democrat Primary
	id = ustates.211
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.211 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	title = { # Liberal democrats founded their own party
		text = ustates.211.t.liberals
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_social_conservatives_democrats
		}
	}
	title = { # Conservative democrats founded their own party
		text = ustates.211.t.conservative
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_market_liberals_democrats
		}
	}

	desc = { # democrats Party won the presidency just last time
		text = ustates.211.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = market_liberal
			has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_democrat
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_democrat }
		}
	}

	desc = { # democrats Party won also in 1940
		text = ustates.211.d.president_steps_down
		trigger = {
			has_government = market_liberal
			has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_democrat
			has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_democrat
		}
	}
	desc = { # democrats Party does not have the Presidency - conservatives split off
		text = ustates.211.d.not_president_conservative
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = market_liberal }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_social_conservatives_democrats }
		}
	}
	desc = { # democrats Party does not have the Presidency
		text = ustates.211.d.not_president_liberal
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = market_liberal }
			has_country_flag = USA_social_conservatives_democrats
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1948_election }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Harry Truman
		name = ustates.211.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_government = market_liberal }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_democrat }
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_democrat
			}
		}

			}

	}
	option = { # President is re-elected

			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_democrat }

country_event = { # 1948 Conservative Democrat Primary
	id = ustates.212

	title = { # Liberal democrats founded their own party

			has_country_flag = USA_social_conservatives_democrats
		}
	}
	title = { # Conservative democrats founded their own party
		text = ustates.212.t.conservative
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_market_liberals_democrats
		}
	}

	desc = { # Democrat Party won the presidency just last time
		text = ustates.212.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_conservative
			has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_democrat
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_democrat }
		}
	}
	desc = { # Democrat Party won also in 1940
		text = ustates.212.d.president_steps_down
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_conservative
			has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_democrat
			has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_democrat
		}

			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_market_liberals_democrats }
		}
	}

			NOT = { has_government = social_conservative }
			has_country_flag = USA_market_liberals_democrats
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election

	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Strom Thurmond

		trigger = {

				NOT = { has_government = social_conservative }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_democrat }
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_democrat
			}
		}

	}
	option = { # Happy Chandler

				NOT = { has_government = social_conservative }

			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_democrat }

	}

country_event = { # 1948 election
	id = ustates.213

	is_triggered_only = yes

		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election

		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1948_election }
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {

						figurehead_president
					}

					traits = {

					}
				}
			}

				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1948_liberal_democrat_primary_truman }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Harry Truman"

### 1952 Elections and Primaries ###
country_event = { # 1952 Progressive Primary
	id = ustates.214
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.214 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.214.t
	desc = { # Progressive Party won the presidency just last time
		text = ustates.214.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_progressive
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive }
		}
	}
	desc = { # Progressive Party won also in 1944
		text = ustates.214.d.president_steps_down
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_progressive
			has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive
		}
	}
	desc = { # Progressive Party does not have the Presidency
		text = ustates.214.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = social_democrat }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_progressives_exist
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1948_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1952_election }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Philip La Follette
		name = ustates.214.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_government = social_democrat }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_progressive }
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1952_progressive_primary_folette
	}
	option = { # Glen H. Taylor
		name = ustates.214.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_government = social_democrat }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_progressive }
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1952_progressive_primary_taylor
	}
	option = { # Keep the Presidency
		name = ustates.214.c
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_progressive
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive }
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1952_progressive_primary_president
	}
}

		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = market_liberal }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1948_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1952_election }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Dwight D. Eisenhower
		name = ustates.216.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_government = market_liberal }
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_democrat
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1952_liberal_primary_eisenhower
	}
	option = { # Adlai Stevenson
		name = ustates.216.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_government = market_liberal }
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_democrat
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1952_liberal_primary_stevenson
	}
	option = { # President is re-elected
		name = ustates.216.c
		trigger = {
			has_government = market_liberal
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_democrat }
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1952_liberal_primary_president
	}
}

country_event = { # 1952 election
	id = ustates.218
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.218 FROM = [From.GetName]" }

	desc = ustates.218.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1948_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1952_election }
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Philip La Follette
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1952_progressive_primary_folette }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Philip La Follette"
					desc = "POLITICS_PHILIP_LA_FOLLETTE_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Philip_La_Follette.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"

					traits = {
						reluctant_interventionist
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Glen H. Taylor
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1952_progressive_primary_taylor }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Glen H. Taylor"
					desc = "POLITICS_GLEN_TAYLOR_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Glen_Taylor.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"

					traits = {
						figurehead_president
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # John W. Bricker
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1952_republican_primary_bricker }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "John W. Bricker"
					desc = "POLITICS_JOHN_BRICKER_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_John_W_Bricker.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_liberal_subtype

						strict_austerity_adherent

				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1952_republican_primary_stassen }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Harold Stassen"
					desc = "POLITICS_HAROLD_STASSEN_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Harold_Stassen.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					traits = {
						tenacious_negotiator
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Dwight D. Eisenhower
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1952_liberal_primary_eisenhower }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Dwight D. Eisenhower"
					desc = "POLITICS_DWIGHT_EISENHOWER_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Dwight_Eisenhower.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = market_liberal_subtype
					traits = {
						great_war_hero
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Adlai Stevenson
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1952_liberal_primary_stevenson }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = " Adlai Stevenson"
					desc = "POLITICS_ADLAI_STEVENSON_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Adlai_Stevenson.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = market_liberal_subtype
					traits = {
						tenacious_negotiator
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # John Sparkman
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1952_conservative_primary_sparkman }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "John Sparkman"
					desc = "POLITICS_JOHN_SPARKMAN_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_John_Sparkman.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_conservative_subtype
					traits = {
						quartermaster_general
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # James Eastland
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1952_conservative_primary_eastland }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "James Eastland"
					desc = "POLITICS_JAMES_EASTLAND_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_James_Eastland.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_conservative_subtype
					traits = {
						divided_interests
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Progressive
		name = ustates.218.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_progressives_exist
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_had_1952_election
		set_country_flag = USA_1952_election_progressive
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat

country_event = { # Join the League?
	id = ustates.250
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.250 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.250.t
	desc = ustates.250.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ustates.250.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = -10
				OR = {
					tag = MEX
					tag = CEN
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -20
				tag = YUC
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		effect_tooltip = { add_ideas = USA_league_of_america_1 }
		FROM = { country_event = ustates.253 }
	}
	option = {
		name = ustates.250.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				OR = {
					tag = MEX
					tag = CEN
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				tag = YUC
			}
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_disapproves_of_govt
		}
		FROM = { country_event = ustates.251 }
	}
}

country_event = { # Change League idea
	id = ustates.255
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.255 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.255.t
	desc = ustates.255.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SWI_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = USA_league_head_3 }
			check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num < 9 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = USA_league_head_2 }
			OR = {
				check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num < 5 }
				check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num > 8 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = USA_league_head_1 }
			OR = {
				check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num < 1 }
				check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num > 4 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num > 0 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ustates.255.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = USA_league_head_3 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num < 1 } }
				remove_ideas = USA_league_head_3
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num < 5 } }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = USA_league_head_3
					add_idea = USA_league_head_1
				}
			}
			else = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = USA_league_head_3
					add_idea = USA_league_head_2
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = USA_league_head_2 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num < 1 } }
				remove_ideas = USA_league_head_2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num > 8 } }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = USA_league_head_2
					add_idea = USA_league_head_3
				}
			}
			else = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = USA_league_head_2
					add_idea = USA_league_head_1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = USA_league_head_1 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num > 8 } }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = USA_league_head_1
					add_idea = USA_league_head_3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num > 4 } }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = USA_league_head_1
					add_idea = USA_league_head_2
				}
			}
			else = {
				remove_ideas = USA_league_head_1
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num > 8 } }
				add_ideas = USA_league_head_3
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num > 4 } }
				add_ideas = USA_league_head_2
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = USA_league_head_1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Removing invalid countries from the league
	id = ustates.259
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.259 FROM = [From.GetName]" }

	title = {
		text = ustates.259.t.league_ends
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { country_exists = USA }
				USA = { is_valid_peace_target = no }
			}
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = ustates.259.t.country_leaves
		trigger = {
			country_exists = USA
			USA = { is_valid_peace_target = yes }
		}
	}

	desc = {
		text = ustates.259.d.USA_dead
		trigger = {
			NOT = { country_exists = USA }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.259.d.USA_puppet
		trigger = {
			USA = { is_subject = yes }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.259.d.USA_in_faction
		trigger = {
			USA = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				is_faction_leader = no
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.259.d.USA_war
		trigger = {

			is_faction_leader = no
			NOT = { is_ally_with = USA }
		}

	desc = {

country_event = { # USA offers advisors
	id = ustates.260
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.260 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.260.t
	desc = ustates.260.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_volunteers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = FROM
			has_idea = USA_american_advisors_1
			has_idea = PSA_american_advisors_1
			has_idea = TEX_american_advisors_1
			has_idea = CSA_american_advisors_1
		}
		OR = {
			has_war_together_with = FROM
			any_enemy_country = {
				has_war_with = FROM
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ustates.260.a # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
		}
		clr_country_flag = USA_offered_advisors
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					tag = USA
				}
			}
			add_ideas = USA_american_advisors_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					tag = PSA
				}
			}
			add_ideas = PSA_american_advisors_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					tag = CSA
				}
			}
			add_ideas = CSA_american_advisors_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					tag = TEX
				}
			}
			add_ideas = TEX_american_advisors_1
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						gives_military_access_to = FROM
						is_in_faction_with = FROM
					}
				}
				give_military_access = FROM
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = ustates.262
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ustates.260.b # Refuse
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 100
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 50
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < 0
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -50
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = ustates.261
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # asking for New England Back
	id = ustates.270
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.270 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.270.t
	desc = ustates.270.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_chicago

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_subject = NEE
			is_in_faction_with = NEE
			any_owned_state = { is_new_england = yes }
		}
	}

	option = { # Lets not risk a war.
		name = ustates.270.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_subject = NEE }
				end_puppet = NEE
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
				NEE = { leave_faction = yes }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = NEE }
				NEE = { separate_peace_all_wars = yes }
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { is_new_england = yes }
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = CAN }
				remove_claim_by = CAN
			}
			FROM = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			set_country_flag = USA_agreed_nee_rejoin
			country_event = ustates.271
		}
	}
	option = { # We shall never give into yankee arrogance
		name = ustates.270.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = CAN_supports_@FROM
					FROM = { has_country_flag = CAN_returned_land }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = CAN_joined_the_ACW
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war = yes
				any_enemy_country = {
					is_actual_major = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				country_exists = GBR
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			set_country_flag = CAN_refused_new_england
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject = no
				}
				effect_tooltip = { leave_faction = yes }
			}
			country_event = ustates.272
		}
	}
}

			}
		}

				limit = { is_in_faction_with = ENT }
				remove_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = KR_trade_sanctions }

			}
		}
	}

		name = ustates.281.b

	}

### Resistance Events ###
country_event = { # Socialist terrorism - factory sabotaged
	id = ustates.400
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.400 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.400.t
	desc = ustates.400.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SRI_bombing

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = USA
			tag = PSA
		}
		OR = {
			has_idea = USA_socialist_resistance1
			has_idea = USA_socialist_resistance2
			has_idea = USA_socialist_resistance3
			has_idea = USA_socialist_resistance4
		}
		any_owned_state = {
			OR = {
				is_core_of = USA
				is_core_of = CSA
				is_core_of = TEX
				is_core_of = PSA
			}
			industrial_complex > 0
			is_controlled_by = ROOT
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			has_idea = USA_socialist_resistance2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_idea = USA_socialist_resistance3
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_idea = USA_socialist_resistance4
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = USA
						is_core_of = CSA
						is_core_of = TEX
						is_core_of = PSA
					}
					industrial_complex > 0
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
				}
				save_event_target_as = attack_state
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ustates.400.a
		add_stability = -0.01
		event_target:attack_state = {
			damage_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				damage = 1.0
			}
			if = {
				limit = { arms_factory > 0 }
				random_list = {
					50 = {
						event_target:attack_state = {
							damage_building = {
								type = arms_factory
								damage = 1.0
							}
						}
					}
					50 = {}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { infrastructure > 3 }
				random_list = {
					25 = {
						event_target:attack_state = {
							damage_building = {
								type = infrastructure
								damage = 2.0
							}
						}
					}
					50 = {
						event_target:attack_state = {
							damage_building = {
								type = infrastructure
								damage = 1.0
							}
						}
					}
					25 = {}
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					ROOT = {
						add_manpower = -3000
					}
				}
				50 = {
					ROOT = {
						add_manpower = -1500
					}
				}
				25 = {
					ROOT = {
						add_manpower = -500
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			base = 40

				factor = 0.5
				has_country_flag = PSA_miss_ceasefire_name
			}

				factor = 0.5
				USA = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = USA_reed_was_president
						has_country_flag = USA_long_was_president
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = PSA_restored_roosevelt
		clr_country_flag = PSA_restored_willkie
		clr_country_flag = PSA_restored_mcnary

		}
	}

		name = ustates.530.b #Yes, let them know we demand MacArthur be imprisoned first

			USA = { NOT = { has_country_flag = Douglas_MacArthur_dead } }

# PSA wants MacArthur Arrested First
country_event = {
	id = ustates.532
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.532 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.532.t
	desc = ustates.532.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_PSA_golden_gate_crowd

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_war_with = PSA }
	}

	option = {
		name = ustates.532.a #For the good of America, let it be done
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_idea = USA_Douglas_MacArthur_hog_sli
				has_idea = USA_Douglas_MacArthur_hog_pau
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				PSA = { has_country_flag = PSA_miss_ceasefire_name }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				PSA = { has_country_flag = PSA_rocky_ceasefire_name }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_republican_primary_macarthur
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_republican_primary_macarthur }
			set_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_garner
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_unit_leader = 56 }
			remove_unit_leader = 56
		}
		set_country_flag = Douglas_MacArthur_dead
		add_political_power = -100
		add_stability = -0.10
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_10 = yes
		PSA = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.534 days = 3 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.539 hours = 5 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ustates.532.b #MacArthur is a hero - refuse
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = USA_reed_was_president
					has_country_flag = USA_long_was_president
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = USA_considering_reunion
		add_political_power = 50
		PSA = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.533 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

		NOT = { has_war_with = USA }
	}

	option = {
		name = ustates.534.a
		clr_country_flag = PSA_restored_roosevelt
		clr_country_flag = PSA_restored_willkie
		clr_country_flag = PSA_restored_mcnary
		hidden_effect = {
			every_navy_leader = { set_nationality = USA }
			every_unit_leader = { set_nationality = USA }
			transfer_navy = { target = USA }
		}
		USA = {
			clr_country_flag = USA_considering_reunion
			annex_country = { target = PSA transfer_troops = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = no }
			USA = { change_tag_from = PSA }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = yes }
				news_event = { id = ustates.536 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = ustates.538.d

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_fired_fourth_of_july }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = { flag = USA_fired_fourth_of_july days = 20 value = 1 }
			country_event = { id = ustates.538 days = 365 }
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { is_american_tag = yes }
				country_event = ustates.538
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ustates.538.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
					NOT = { has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_begun_flag }
				}
			}
			add_political_power = 5
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -10
		}
	}
}

	desc = ustates.624.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_bombing_run

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				tag = USA
				has_war_with = TEX
				has_war_with = CSA
			}
			AND = {
				tag = TEX
				has_war_with = USA
				has_war_with = CSA
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 2
	}

	option = {# Yes
		name = ustates.624.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		if = {
			limit = {
				TEX = {
					exists = yes
				}
				NOT = { tag = TEX }
			}
			TEX = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = USA_fire_bombings
					days = 90
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				USA = {
					exists = yes
				}
				NOT = { tag = USA }
			}
			USA = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = USA_fire_bombings
					days = 90
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CSA = {
					exists = yes
				}
			}
			CSA = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = USA_fire_bombings
					days = 90
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {# No
		name = ustates.624.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}
}

		clr_country_flag = added_AI_strategies_@FROM
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = prepare_for_war
			id = FROM
			value = -1000
		}
		FROM = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = prepare_for_war
				id = FROM
				value = -1000
			}
		}
	}
}

		name = ustates.660.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.661
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # We shall never give into yankee arrogance
		name = ustates.660.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				any_enemy_country = { is_actual_major = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				strength_ratio = { tag = FROM ratio < 0.2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = CAN_supports_@FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				country_exists = GBR
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			set_country_flag = USA_refused_panama
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.662
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

# American Civil War
news_event = {
	id = ustates.1000
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.1000 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ustates.1000.t
	picture = GFX_news_event_USA_second_american_civil_war

	desc = {
		text = ustates.1000.d.all
		trigger = {
			country_exists = CSA
			country_exists = TEX
			country_exists = PSA
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.1000.d.nocal
		trigger = {
			country_exists = CSA
			country_exists = TEX
			NOT = { country_exists = PSA }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.1000.d.csa
		trigger = {
			country_exists = CSA
			NOT = { country_exists = TEX }
			NOT = { country_exists = PSA }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.1000.d.aus
		trigger = {
			NOT = { country_exists = CSA }
			country_exists = TEX
			NOT = { country_exists = PSA }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		wants_world_news = yes
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	show_major = {
		NOT = {
			tag = USA
			tag = CSA
			tag = TEX
			tag = PSA
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ustates.1000.a
	}
}
